5  Krill MSE Application

A naive application of a Management Strategy Evaluation to the Krill Fishery

5.1 Introduction

5.2 Run MSE

5.2.1 Build the Operating Model

# Selecting scenario "scn-2", as it's composed by the PR scenario providing
# estimates of M closest to range in Pakhomov (1995), and maturity ogive based
# on estimates recommended in Maschette et al (2021)
krill_pars <- grym_setups |> 
  filter(scenario_id == "scn-2")
  
krill_OM <- build_krill_OM(
  om_name = "krill_demo", maxage = last(unlist(krill_pars$Ages)), 
  Linf = krill_pars$Linf, K = krill_pars$K, t0 = krill_pars$t0, 
  mat50Min = krill_pars$mat50Min, mat50Max = krill_pars$mat50Max, 
  matrange = krill_pars$matrange, 
  sel50Min = krill_pars$sel50Min, sel50Max = krill_pars$sel50Min, 
  selrange = krill_pars$selrange,
  a = krill_pars$a, b = krill_pars$b, 
  M_draws = krill_pars$prRecruitPars$`PR-emm21`$M, 
  RCV_draws = krill_pars$prRecruitPars$`PR-emm21`$CV, 
  n_iter = krill_pars$n_iter, proj_yrs = krill_pars$n.years, 
  maxF = krill_pars$Fmax, seed = 10001
)

Harvest control rules for data limited stocks using length-based reference points and survey biomass indices

5.2.2 Specify Management Procedures

source("krill_mse_metrics.R")

krill_OM@nsim <- 250

krill_OM@interval <- 1

krill_OM@D <- c(0.7, 1.1)

krill_OM@LenCV <- c(0.05, 0.1)


krill_OM@CAL_nsamp <- c(800, 1500)
krill_OM@CAL_ESS <- c(400, 750)

krill_OM@Cobs <- c(0, 0)
krill_OM@Iobs <- c(0.01, 1)


# run historical period
krill_hist <- Simulate(krill_OM)

5.2.3 Performance Metrics

Metrics related to Spawning Biomass

CCAMLR’s Defaults
summary(krill_mse, c("PD", "ESC"))
Calculating Performance Metrics 
                                  Performance.Metrics 
1  Depletion: Spawning Stock Biomass relative to SSB0 
2 Escapement: Final Spawning Biomass relative to SSB0 
                                          
1 Prob. min(SSB) < 0.2 SSB0 (Years 1 - 20)
2      median(SSB at Year 20)/median(SSB0)


Performance Statistics:
     MP    PD  ESC
1   AvC 0.068 0.77
2 BK_ML 0.870 0.21
3   ITM 0.900 0.15
SSB relative to unfished dynamic SSB
projyrs_idx <- (krill_mse@nyears+1)

Y <- krill_mse@nyears+krill_mse@proyears

ssb_f0 <- krill_mse@RefPoint$Dynamic_Unfished$SSB0[, (krill_mse@nyears+1):Y] 
ssb <- krill_mse@SSB
dim(ssb)
[1] 250   3  20
dim(ssb_f0)
[1] 250  20
ssb_ssbf0 <- apply(ssb, 2, function(x){ x/ssb_f0 }, simplify = FALSE)
lapply(ssb_ssbf0, function(x) x < 0.2)

ssb_unfished <- krill_mse@RefPoint$Dynamic_Unfished$SSB0[, (krill_mse@nyears+1):Y] %>%
  reshape2::melt() |> 
  rename(sim = Var1, year = Var2, ssb_f0 = value)

ssb <- reshape2::melt(krill_mse@SSB) |>
  rename(sim = Var1, MP = Var2, year = Var3, ssb = value) |> 
  right_join(ssb_unfished)
Joining with `by = join_by(sim, year)`
# ssb %>%
#   group_by(year, MP) |> 
#   summarise(med_ssb = median(ssb), .groups = "keep") |> 
#   ggplot(aes(x = year, y = med_ssb, colour = factor(MP))) +
#   geom_line()


ssb |>
  mutate(below25pct = ssb < 0.2 * ssb_f0) |> 
  group_by(sim, MP) |> 
  summarise(streak = ifelse(sum(below25pct) != 0, with(rle(below25pct), max(lengths[values])), 0 ), .groups = "keep") |> 
  ggplot(aes(x = factor(MP), y = streak)) +
  ggdist::stat_halfeye() +
  labs(y = "Max nr. consecutive years with SSB < 0.2 * SSB_f0")

ssb |> 
  group_by(MP, sim) |> 
  summarise(min_ssb_v_ssbf0 = min(ssb/ssb_f0), .groups = "drop_last") |> 
  summarise(p = mean(min_ssb_v_ssbf0 < 0.2))
ssb |> 
  mutate(ssb_v_ssbf0 = ssb < 0.2 * ssb_f0) |> 
  group_by(MP) |> 
  summarise(p = mean(ssb_v_ssbf0))
ssb |> 
  mutate(ssb_v_ssbf0 = ssb < 0.2 * ssb_f0) |> 
  group_by(MP, sim) |> 
  summarise(p = mean(ssb_v_ssbf0), .groups = "drop_last") |> 
  summarise(mean(p))
ssb |> 
  mutate(ssb_v_ssbf0 = ssb < 0.2 * ssb_f0) |> 
  group_by(MP, sim) |> 
  summarise(p = mean(ssb_v_ssbf0), .groups = "drop_last") |> 
  pivot_wider(names_from = MP, values_from = p)
